981:     var binary = atob(value);
982:     var out = new Uint8Array(binary.length);
983:     for (var i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) out[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i);
984:     return out;
985:   }

981:     var binary = atob(value);

974:   function bytesToBase64(bytes) {
975:     var binary = '';
976:     for (var i = 0; i < bytes.length; i++) binary += String.fromCharCode(bytes[i]);
977:     return btoa(binary);

980:   function base64ToBytes(value) {
981:     var binary = atob(value);
982:     var out = new Uint8Array(binary.length);
983:     for (var i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) out[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i);
984:     return out;

981:     var binary = atob(value);
982:     var out = new Uint8Array(binary.length);
983:     for (var i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) out[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i);
